  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c777af04-829d-4f37-b353-a63b69368fea'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText15233550121790363014" style="display:none"><b>He's Playing Games</b><br /><br />Though Rylann Pierce tried to fight the sparks she felt for billionaire heir Kyle Rhodes the night they met, their sizzling chemistry was undeniable. But after being stood up on their first date, Rylann never expected to see him again. So when she finds herself face-to-face with Kyle in a courthouse nine years later, she's stunned. More troubling to the beautiful assistant U.S. attorney is that she's still wildly attracted to him.<br /><br /><b>But She's Making The Rules</b><br /><br />Just released from prison, Kyle Rhodes isn't thrilled to be the star witness in a high-profile criminal case—but when Rylann comes knocking at his door, he finds she may be the one lawyer he can't say no to. Still as gorgeous and sharp-tongued as ever, she lays down the law: she doesn't mix business with pleasure. But Kyle won't give up on something he wants—and what he wants is the one woman he's never forgotten.</span>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/1731495-karli">Karli</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The first 2 will give you background and info about some characters, but it's not necessary to understand and enjoy this book. I read #1 then #3 becau<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The first 2 will give you background and info about some characters, but it's not necessary to understand and enjoy this book. I read #1 then #3 because that's what my library had. Now that #2 and #4 are here, I'm reading them. My only problem is remembering the first 2 I read because it was so long ago, not that they were out of order.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

She's actually not all that amazing personality-wise. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601376854ra/30167506.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Regardless, what adult calls another adult <i>sassy</i>?   <span id="freeText7234370439571496057" style="display:none">I liked the characters <i>well enough</i> and the storyline was actually pretty fun. But the DIALOGUE. So horrible.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601377108ra/30167540.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's <i>sassy</i>. He just keeps repeating that she's so sassy. <br>But she's not actually sassy. She just sort of didn't fall all over herself to sleep with him right away. That's it. She's actually not all that amazing personality-wise. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601376854ra/30167506.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Regardless, what adult calls another adult <i>sassy</i>? Much less over and over? I guess billionaires fantasize about sassy women or something. &lt;--did I mention he's a billionaire?<br>Because he is. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601376854ra/30167507.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know, just casually. It doesn't play into the story much, other than he doesn't have to eat Ramen noodles and he has one of those idiotic cars with doors that open upward like it has wings. Because those don't look pretentious and stupid as fuck or anything.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601376854ra/30167508.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Plus, I don't know, it's like we're supposed to think he's <i>hard</i> because he's an ex-con. Ok. He was in prison for 6 months. For HACKING TWITTER. And there's this one scene where he 'scares' these young hackers with his dweeby prison stories. Ahahaha!<br>Get outta here. 6 months for hacking Twitter does <i>not</i> a tough guy make.<br>And she asked him if he <i>worked out every day</i> while he was in prison to explain his nice body. &lt;--stop it. just stop it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601376854ra/30167509.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So.<br>Supposedly, he's this brilliant computer genius, heir to a billion-dollar fortune, a tough ex-con, and still pining over her from the ONE time they met in a bar back in college and he walked her home.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1601375297ra/30167433.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also.<br><b>Assistant District Attorney.</b> &lt;--we get it. It's your job title.<br>There was really no need for that <b>full title</b> to be repeated ad nauseam throughout the book.<br><i>He thought she was a great Assistant District Attorney.<br>She loved her job as an Assistant District Attorney.<br>He realized he was talking to the Assistant District Attorney.<br>Sorry, I have to take this call because I'm an Assistant District Attorney.</i><br>Jesus Christ, cut it out! <br>And all the lawyer puns? Ohmyfuckinggod. Lawyers don't sit around making references like <i>I'll plead the 5th</i> to their other lawyer friends. <br>I used to love Julie James but this...? The dialogue was ridonkulously cheesy and just killed what could have been a cute story for me.<br><br>I listened to the audiobook and it did <i>nothing</i> to alleviate the pain of getting through this one. Blech.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7234370439571496057" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_245258614" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/245258614" />
    <a title="Erika" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6721219-erika"><img alt="Erika" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511329430p2/6721219.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245258614?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erika" href="/user/show/6721219-erika">Erika</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101561379" href="/book/show/12832257-about-that-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=auto-buy-author">auto-buy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=outstanding-characters">outstanding-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=ladies-of-quality">ladies-of-quality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=best-of-heroes">best-of-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6721219-erika?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245258614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4929422145051541981"><i>"There are some things a girl never forgets, Ry. And one of those is a kiss from a right guy."</i><br/><br/>There are some things I know I would likely find in Julie James's books.<br/>1. No TSTL heroine<br/>2. Informative stuffs<br/>3. Hilarity<br/>4. Great supporting characters<br/>5. No unnecessary misunderstandings in romance<br/><br/><i>About That Night</i> is no exception. Rylann Pierce aka Prosecutrix Pierce and Kyle Rhodes aka Smug Dimples are two down to earth characters. Rylann was a typical Julie James's heroine. Strong, independent, ambit</span>
  <span id="freeText4929422145051541981" style="display:none"><i>"There are some things a girl never forgets, Ry. And one of those is a kiss from a right guy."</i><br><br>There are some things I know I would likely find in Julie James's books.<br>1. No TSTL heroine<br>2. Informative stuffs<br>3. Hilarity<br>4. Great supporting characters<br>5. No unnecessary misunderstandings in romance<br><br><i>About That Night</i> is no exception. Rylann Pierce aka Prosecutrix Pierce and Kyle Rhodes aka Smug Dimples are two down to earth characters. Rylann was a typical Julie James's heroine. Strong, independent, ambitious, and smart. While Kyle... well, he's something. <br><br>Smug Dimples wasn't like what I expected him to be. Knowing him from the previous book had given me the impression of a hero like Jason in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3863861-just-the-sexiest-man-alive?utm_medium=api&amp;utm_source=blog_book" rel="nofollow noopener">Just the Sexiest Man Alive</a>. I had thought I would find a charming but spoil rich guy with some boyish attitude. I was right, but only with the charming and rich parts. <br><br>It was very interesting to witness how the perfect life of a billionaire heir became not so perfect anymore because of one brilliant but stupid action. The most interesting part is the way he's living it. I was amazed by the transformation of Kyle Rhodes from a fresh graduated college boy, to a Twitter terrorist, to an ex-con, and to a man who starts his own empire. I adored how he took his responsibility as a son and a brother. I was impressed with the way he dealt with his past mistake and did something right with it. <br><br>So, what's not to like about a book that made me learn some valuable things? I would have rated it more than 5 stars if the book had been titled with something like <i>The life of Kyle Rhodes</i>. The problem was, this is a romance. I liked Smug Dimples and Prosecutrix Pierce together. They are two grown up and broad minded people with a huge-9-years-old-crush on each other. They made me laugh often, and not so often I wanted to strangle them both. But for a romance book, the romance itself was not enough. It needed to be explored more. I wanted to see more Kyle and Rylann together.<br><br>Overall, despite it wasn't a great romance to me, I thought it was a great book. Lots of messages in it. From all five books by the author, Kyle may not be the best hero, but he's the best character. You'll probably find the romance isn't satisfying, still there are heartwarming family bonds and friendships. You'll be entertained with lovable characters. I was so happy to find Jack (my baby), Cameron, Nick, and Jordan. Also Kyle and Jordan's father, Rae the best friend, Sam Wilkins. Oh I can't mention them all. Julie James is great in creating supporting characters, those people who can make you feel like you're talking and joking with them because they are great together. Thus, I wasn't satisfied with the romance, but I wasn't disappointed with the book. And I just can't wait for more books by Julie James. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380364660i/716421.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>The smugness of baby Kyle's dimples ;)</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4929422145051541981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_217508713" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/217508713" />
    <a title="Dija" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2857113-dija"><img alt="Dija" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360335537p2/2857113.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/217508713?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dija" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dija" href="/user/show/2857113-dija">Dija</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=awww">awww</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=cr">cr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=authors-i-stalk">authors-i-stalk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=cotton-candy-fluff">cotton-candy-fluff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=my-reviews">my-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=wow">wow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=apr-2012">apr-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer217508713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9114647102612926295">Julie James makes me want to throw my psychology degree out the window and try out for law school instead. If all this sass and bad-assery is what they teach in law, sign me up!<br/><br/>After having read all of JJ's published novels so far, there are several things I've come to expect from her:<br/><br/><b>1.</b> Confident, bold, and yummy heroes whose jobs or pasts involve the law in some way. <br/><b>2. </b> Sarcastic, spirited, and driven heroines who're usually attorneys. <br/><b>3. </b> Great sexual chemistry between the H&h which never le</span>
  <span id="freeText9114647102612926295" style="display:none">Julie James makes me want to throw my psychology degree out the window and try out for law school instead. If all this sass and bad-assery is what they teach in law, sign me up!<br><br>After having read all of JJ's published novels so far, there are several things I've come to expect from her:<br><br><b>1.</b> Confident, bold, and yummy heroes whose jobs or pasts involve the law in some way. <br><b>2. </b> Sarcastic, spirited, and driven heroines who're usually attorneys. <br><b>3. </b> Great sexual chemistry between the H&amp;h which never leads to an anticlimactic resolution. <br><b>4.</b> A fabulous cast of supporting characters who add more life to the novel than anything else.<br><b>5.</b> No drawn-out, prolonged drama whatsoever. These stories are fast-paced, realistic, natural, and long enough to be neither tedious nor abrupt, but just right.<br><br>James delivers on all five accounts again, and then some. <i>About That Night</i> has everything I've come to expect from her romances, which basically comes down to me smiling throughout the entire novel. Seriously, my cheeks hurt from all the grinning. <br><br>After being humiliated on and dumped through Twitter, computer-whiz Kyle shuts down the site for two days. As expected, he gets caught and sent to prison, thereafter becoming globally infamous as the Twitter Terrorist. After four months in jail, his sister, Jordan, works out a deal with the FBI to reduce his sentence to time served. <br><br>Ambitious Rylann comes to Chicago as an Assistant U.S. Attorney and her first case involves Kyle. To say sparks fly when the two meet again after their brief meeting nine years ago would be a <i>huge</i> understatement. The dynamic relationship between Kyle and Rylann starts as soon as they set eyes on each other and it only gets progressively hotter and steamier. <br><br>As an added bonus, there are plenty of scenes with Jack, Cameron, Jordan, and Nick that clearly show how their respective relationships have developed during the intermissions. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I hope we can get to see at least one of their weddings in the upcoming books. I'd love reading the details of <i>that</i>! Especially since none of the books in this series have an epilogue. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There's not a thing about the story I would change, but being the cover-obsessed freak I am, I can't help but wish that Rylann had been wearing a hot dress on the cover instead of the suit; the red one she wore in the book would have been rather fitting. Other than that, <i>About That Night</i> is the perfect sequel to <i>A Lot Like Love</i>, and I can't wait to see which couple will be introduced next. If I were to hazard a guess, my top choice would be <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Rae and Sam <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. There's definitely a story there, and I can't wait to read it.<br><br><b>Kyle:</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360361i/711203.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b>Rylann:</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360361i/711204.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b><i>Some</i> of my favorite quotes:</b><br><blockquote>
<b>#1:</b> Kyle gazed down at her. “I lied when I said I followed you to the bar because you’re hot.” He touched her cheek. “I saw you laughing with your friends, and your smile sucked me right in.”<br><br><b>#2:</b> "There are some things a girl never forgets, Ry. And one of those is a kiss from the right guy."<br><br><b>#3:</b> Much to his surprise, she actually blushed.<br>Well, well. Apparently the unflappable Prosecutrix Pierce could be…flapped after all.<br>Interesting.<br><br><b>#4:</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And even if she didn’t say a single word more, Kyle knew he would never again doubt the way Rylann felt about him.<br>She was wearing his flannel shirt.<br>“You kept it,” he said softly. “All this time.”<br>She nodded. “For nine years, I’ve held on to this darn shirt, literally dragging it across the country and back.”<br>Kyle touched her cheek, gently brushing away a tear with his thumb. “Why?”<br>She paused hesitantly, and then with a tender smile, finally put it all on the line, too. “I guess I always hoped you’d come back for it someday.” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
</blockquote> <br>4.5/5 stars<br><br><b>For more reviews, visit my <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>. </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/164751010?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of witty, fun, steamy contemporary romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-prim-proper-decorous">heroine-prim-proper-decorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=author-julie-james">author-julie-james</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hh-lawyers-ex-lawyers-need-love">hh-lawyers-ex-lawyers-need-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-miss-independent">heroine-miss-independent</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=best-snarkasm-humor">best-snarkasm-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hh-famous-celebrity">hh-famous-celebrity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-career-professional-success">heroine-career-professional-success</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-bedroom-bad-boy">hero-bedroom-bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer164751010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5359823833689950236">5 stars – Contemporary Romance<br/><br/>I’m an avid Julie James fangirl and I love her snappy, clever, banterific dialogue and snarky humor. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5082599.Practice_Makes_Perfect' title='Practice Makes Perfect by Julie James' rel='nofollow noopener'>Practice Makes Perfect</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6642402.Something_About_You__FBI___US_Attorney____1_' title='Something About You (FBI / US Attorney, # 1) by Julie James' rel='nofollow noopener'>Something About You</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___US_Attorney___2_' title='A Lot Like Love (FBI / US Attorney, #2) by Julie James' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Lot Like Love</a> were some of my favorite reads of last year, and I’ve been eagerly awaiting Kyle’s story.<br/> <br/>Although I didn’t enjoy <i>
  <b>About That Night</b>
</i> as much as the previous books in the <i>FBI/US Attorney</i> series, it’s still an entertaining, satisfying read. The romance between sexy computer genius Kyle Rhodes, aka “Smug</span>
  <span id="freeText5359823833689950236" style="display:none">5 stars – Contemporary Romance<br><br>I’m an avid Julie James fangirl and I love her snappy, clever, banterific dialogue and snarky humor. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5082599.Practice_Makes_Perfect" title="Practice Makes Perfect by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">Practice Makes Perfect</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6642402.Something_About_You__FBI___US_Attorney____1_" title="Something About You (FBI / US Attorney, # 1) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">Something About You</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___US_Attorney___2_" title="A Lot Like Love (FBI / US Attorney, #2) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">A Lot Like Love</a> were some of my favorite reads of last year, and I’ve been eagerly awaiting Kyle’s story.<br> <br>Although I didn’t enjoy <i>
  <b>About That Night</b>
</i> as much as the previous books in the <i>FBI/US Attorney</i> series, it’s still an entertaining, satisfying read. The romance between sexy computer genius Kyle Rhodes, aka “Smug Dimples,” “Twitter Terrorist”, and Sawyer from <i>Lost</i> lookalike, and sassy law geek, “counselor”, “Meth Lab” Rylann, aka “Prosecutrix Pierce” and “brunette bombshell”, was highly amusing and steamy. These two ignited some serious sparks! I would have liked a bit more to the ending and an epilogue, but overall I really enjoyed it! 5 stars!<br><br>And who would have figured cyber geek Kyle for such a bedroom bad boy and smokin’ hot dirty talker?!?! Yowza!<br><br>This scene cracked me up.<br><br><i>“I don’t mind hot and spicy. Actually find that appealing in a girl.” He cocked his head, thinking this over. “And chicken wings.” Rylann turned her head and stared at him. “Did you really just compare me to chicken wings?” “You say that like it’s a bad thing. Chicken wings are the bomb.”</i><br><br>Kyle<br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=Josh-Holloway-Lost.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220129040" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220129040?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=z-audiobooks">z-audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=self-contained">self-contained</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220129040" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10604362060018913517">~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br/><b>
  <blockquote>“There are some things a girl never forgets, Ry. And one of those is a kiss from the right guy” </blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383232373i/6450387._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This was a fabulous read! I'm still excited a day after I finished it. I "read" the audio. My rating for the narrator is about a 3.5-4 stars. My rating for the book, 4.5 stars.<br/><br/>So the premise is really about two things: <br/><u>1. The night that Ryland and Kyle meet, kiss, and then separate for nine years<br/>2. How Kyle Rhodes became the "Twitter Terrorist" and an ex con</u><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10604362060018913517" style="display:none">~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><b>
  <blockquote>“There are some things a girl never forgets, Ry. And one of those is a kiss from the right guy” </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383232373i/6450387._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This was a fabulous read! I'm still excited a day after I finished it. I "read" the audio. My rating for the narrator is about a 3.5-4 stars. My rating for the book, 4.5 stars.<br><br>So the premise is really about two things: <br><u>1. The night that Ryland and Kyle meet, kiss, and then separate for nine years<br>2. How Kyle Rhodes became the "Twitter Terrorist" and an ex con</u><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I don’t mind hot and spicy. Actually find that appealing in a girl. And chicken wings.”</blockquote>
</b><br>** Rylann Pierce and Kyle Rhodes met at a bar, feel an instant connection, share some witty banter, and then share a romantic and hot kiss after Kyle walks Rylann home. But then Rylann is left hanging the next day while waiting for Kyle to show up for their planned date. She's a tiny bit brokenhearted because she could have sworn there was a deep connection between them, but life goes on...<br><br>Rylann completes her college degree, becomes a US Attorney, and enjoys her relationship with her longtime boyfriend, fully expecting that her life is on a steady path toward fulfillment.<br><br>Kyle helps to run his father's multimillion dollar computer security company, enjoying the freedoms that come with being rich and the women who flock to him. But somewhere along the line, the empty relationships begin to feel hollow. Sensing that he might need to settle down and create something lasting, Kyle latches on to his current fling, a gorgeous model type, and is then shocked and horrified when she breaks up with him months later...via Twitter.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383232373i/6450388._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Mortified and angry, a humiliated Kyle utilizes his computer hacking skills to shut down the social media site for two days...until he realizes that he is in big...freaking...trouble. Kyle serves his time in jail but resents the prosecutor's office that labeled him the "Twitter Terrorist". It was just Twitter, for goodness sake. And then at a hearing for an early release, who walks in the courtroom but his nine years gone dream woman, Rylann Pierce. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402240i/781681.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And the games begin...<br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br><b>
  <u>MY THOUGHTS:</u>
</b><br>Just like Julie James other books, this is a funny and clever contemporary romance. Not a lot of drama, just the story of how two people meant to be end up meshing their lives together when it seems that so many obstacles are in their way. Their sexual tension is more than palpable...<br><b>
  <blockquote>“Her body trembled as she finally caved. “Touch me, Kyle. Now,” she begged.<br>Thank fucking God.”</blockquote>
</b> <br>The conflict is that Rylann is a US Attorney and Kyle is an ex con. Not to mention, it was Rylann's office that prosecuted Kyle and gave him his infamous label. Not to fear...Kyle gives Rylann her own label. She's his "Prosecutrix Pierce." :D:D Cracked me up every time. <br><br>I love the time of life that these two are in...both grown up but searching for permanence. And they just fit together so well, complimented each other when they were together. Their relationship felt very natural. <br><b>
  <blockquote>“Because nine years ago, I walked up to the most beautiful girl in the bar, and tonight she's still the only person I want to talk to.” </blockquote>
</b></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/164086423" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/164086423?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-contemporary-romance">genre-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-julie-james">author-julie-james</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer164086423" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13427211767262865455"><b>Posted on<a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/04/arc-review-about-that-night-by-julie.html' rel='nofollow noopener'></a> Under the Covers</b><br/><br/>An unforgettable kiss started it all...<br/><br/>Nine years ago, Rylann Pierce, a sweet girl with big dreams met a billionaire heir named Kyle Rhodes. They talked, sparks ignited. Kyle walked her home like a perfect gentleman, leaving her breathless after one kiss and a promise to see her again the next day.<br/><br/>But when Kyle is a no-show the next day, Rylann decides that dating a billionaire heir isn’t in her six-year plan. So she busies herself, working on her career until she becom</span>
  <span id="freeText13427211767262865455" style="display:none"><b>Posted on<a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/04/arc-review-about-that-night-by-julie.html" rel="nofollow noopener"></a> Under the Covers</b><br /><br />An unforgettable kiss started it all...<br /><br />Nine years ago, Rylann Pierce, a sweet girl with big dreams met a billionaire heir named Kyle Rhodes. They talked, sparks ignited. Kyle walked her home like a perfect gentleman, leaving her breathless after one kiss and a promise to see her again the next day.<br /><br />But when Kyle is a no-show the next day, Rylann decides that dating a billionaire heir isn’t in her six-year plan. So she busies herself, working on her career until she becomes an Assistant US Attorney.<br /><br />Fast-forward years later and Rylann gets the gig she’s been dreaming of. But her first case isn’t ideal because she comes face-to-face with Kyle Rhodes once again, still fully equipped with those big blue eyes, cute dimples, snarky remarks and shampoo commercial hair. To reiterate, she is screwed . Because all those repressed feelings for Kyle return in a flood.<br /><br />ABOUT THAT NIGHT brings in the sizzling tension in truckloads. I loved Kyle in A LOT LIKE LOVE. But Julie James really does deliver a stellar book for our favourite Twitter Terrorist. Readers can expect more of what they loved in the previous books of this series – great characters, impeccable knowledge of courtroom antics, and the perfect blend of sweet, sexy and funny.<br /><br />However, I have to say that Kyle seems to bring a little more sexiness to this book. Perhaps out of all of James’ books so far, ABOUT THAT NIGHT is the steamiest! Kyle likes to talk some filth! So prepare for some swooning.<br /><br />Rylann was a perfect match for him, meeting him head-to-head with her witty comebacks. It was a pleasure to read a strong heroine who knew what she wanted in life, even if she wasn’t sure how she was going to reach it. While it takes her awhile for her to decide that what she really needs in a blue-eyed looker (don’t we all?), Rylann does come to terms with her feelings for Kyle eventually.<br /><br />There was a good amount of angst in this one, though it wasn’t bitter and that was very important for me. I felt like if Rylann stayed bitter about being left high and dry the entire time, this would have been disastrous. Instead, it shined because bitterness and humor don’t always mix so well.<br /><br />Followers of this series will be thrilled to note that there are many familiar faces in this book. Cameron Lynde, the heroine from SOMETHING ABOUT YOU, makes an early appearance as Rylann’s boss. The hero and heroine of A LOT LIKE LOVE, Jordan, Kyle’s sister and Nick McCall also have considerable airtime. Of course, we can’t forget Wilkins, Jack’s partner who plays a huge role in this book and Jack Pallas is there as well.<br /><br />I wonder who will get a book next!<br /><br />*ARC provided by publisher </span>
  <a data-text-id="13427211767262865455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer229978918" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16508027441560395569"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>When I think of a classy adult romance, Julie James always comes to mind. I loved the first two of the FBI /US Attorney series, and for the most part I enjoyed this one as well. <br/><br/>Rylann Pierce is a US Assistant Attorney just moved from San Francisco to Chicago back to her roots after a breakup. One of her first cases is a “time-served” early release case of Kyle Rhodes, “the Twitter Terrorist.” This is a little awkward because it just so happens that nine years ago Rylann and Kyle shared</span>
  <span id="freeText16508027441560395569" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />When I think of a classy adult romance, Julie James always comes to mind. I loved the first two of the FBI /US Attorney series, and for the most part I enjoyed this one as well. <br /><br />Rylann Pierce is a US Assistant Attorney just moved from San Francisco to Chicago back to her roots after a breakup. One of her first cases is a “time-served” early release case of Kyle Rhodes, “the Twitter Terrorist.” This is a little awkward because it just so happens that nine years ago Rylann and Kyle shared a few passionate kisses in college, but lost track of each other after a family tragedy got in the way. Neither one forgot the other, but they never thought they’d cross paths again. Fate had other plans. <br /><br />Kyle Rhodes, a computer genius and billionaire, has just been released after an agreement orchestrated by his sister, Jordan, and her FBI boyfriend (we had their story in the previous novel). He drunkenly hacked into Twitter and shut the site down after a very public breakup. Very stupid move over a girl he barely cared about, but he paid dearly. Imagine his surprise when he lays eyes on a sassy brunette he let get away. Now that Rylann is on his radar again he can’t get her out of his mind. A case brings them back together, but complications arise from their situation; Kyle was convicted in a highly publicized trial by the very office Rylann now works for and a relationship could call question to her position. <br /><br />I really enjoyed Kyle and Rylann’s relationship. It’s grown up, without frustrating drama and incredibly sweet. They shared sizzling scenes filled with chemistry and swoon. As I said, I’m a fan of Julie James and her classy romances, but this one seemed to lack the usual spark. First of all, we only get Kyle and Rylann together for a snippet in the beginning and then for what felt like half* of the story they’re off living their own lives on different paths. Also, in each of the two previous stories there was a danger and suspense element that lent excitement to the story. About That Night did not have that. There is no underlying threat or mystery to solve driving the plot. <br /><br />I “read” the audio-version of About That Night. The narration took me a while to get into because of the narrator’s style of delivery. I’m not sure how to describe it other than there was pausing throughout the delivery that I thought was a little much. I did get used to it eventually, but I’d listen to a sample of this story before I bought it just to see if it works for you. <br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I don’t mind hot and spicy. Actually find that appealing in a girl … And chicken wings.”<br />Rylann turned her head and stared at him. “Did you really just compare me to chicken wings?”<br />“You say that like it’s a bad thing. Chicken wings are the bomb.”<br /><br />“You came along and changed everything. I don’t want to be some guy you’re fooling around with anymore, Rylann. I want to be with you all the way.”</i>
</b><br /><br />*It’s hard to determine if it was actually half of the story because I was listening to the audio-version.<br /><br />You can read this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2013/08/review-about-that-night-by-julie-james.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16508027441560395569" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2749916054" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/18469437-about-that-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=audible-escape">audible-escape</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2019">2019</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2749916054" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8189669051654209461">A fun series of standalone books. This featured Kyle, the brother of Jordan from book 2 and Ryland, a new character to the series.<br/><br/>Kyle is fresh out of prison for hacking twitter and shutting it down for 24 hours. The previous DA pushed for maximum sentence due to his father's billionaire status. In book 2, he was released early after his sister made a deal with the new DA if she helped the FBI get into an exclusive wine party to plant bugs in the owners office.<br/><br/>Kyle and Ryland met for only one ni</span>
  <span id="freeText8189669051654209461" style="display:none">A fun series of standalone books. This featured Kyle, the brother of Jordan from book 2 and Ryland, a new character to the series.<br /><br />Kyle is fresh out of prison for hacking twitter and shutting it down for 24 hours. The previous DA pushed for maximum sentence due to his father's billionaire status. In book 2, he was released early after his sister made a deal with the new DA if she helped the FBI get into an exclusive wine party to plant bugs in the owners office.<br /><br />Kyle and Ryland met for only one night, 9 years ago when they were still in college. They were supposed to go on a date the next night but Kyle found out his mother was in an accident and he had to go home. The attraction they felt is still there after 9 years but now Ryland is an ADA in the office where Kyle was convicted. <br /><br />I liked Ryland but she was a bit too by the book at times. Kyle was ok for me. I think I just couldn't get past the younger brother version of him we saw in Jordan's book. I still very, much enjoyed the writing and was entertained by this audiobook. I borrowed this on the Audio Romance Package and love the narrator. She does a fantastic job.</span>

<div id="review_246519927" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/246519927" />
    <a title="Mimi Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith"><img alt="Mimi Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297016674p2/4884889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/246519927?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4884889-mimi-smith?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer246519927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7773599596068675771"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>Facts are:</b><br/><br/>Julie James publishes ONE book a year<br/>Julie James is a great writer<br/>I love Julie James's books, but...<br/>...for one book a year they're way too short.<br/><br/>Basically, I LOVED this book, and everything about it, but I just wanted MORE. More of the relationship development, Kyle, everything, KYLE...<br/>The humor in these books is amazing...<br/><br/><i>"Rae shifted her position to check out the object of their discussion. “If that’s the new face of computer geek, sign me up. He can push my keyboard buttons</i></span>
  <span id="freeText7773599596068675771" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>Facts are:</b><br /><br />Julie James publishes ONE book a year<br />Julie James is a great writer<br />I love Julie James's books, but...<br />...for one book a year they're way too short.<br /><br />Basically, I LOVED this book, and everything about it, but I just wanted MORE. More of the relationship development, Kyle, everything, KYLE...<br />The humor in these books is amazing...<br /><br /><i>"Rae shifted her position to check out the object of their discussion. “If that’s the new face of computer geek, sign me up. He can push my keyboard buttons any day.”<br /><br />Rylann turned her head and stared at him. “Did you really just compare me to chicken wings?”<br />“You say that like it’s a bad thing. Chicken wings are the bomb.”<br /><br />“Oh God, that hurts,” she whimpered.<br />“What hurts?” Kyle asked, sounding concerned.<br />“The invisible man pounding spikes into my head.”<br />“That doesn’t sound good. Maybe you should take out an invisible Taser gun and zap the son of a bitch.”</i><br /><br />I adore Kyle, he's perfect!<br /><br /><i>"Kyle warily eyed the two FBI agents—yes, now there were two; apparently they multiplied like wet gremlins—as they pushed open the red privacy curtain and entered the theater box."</i><br /><br />The infamous Twitter terrorist is a hunk. And a geek extraodinare After getting drunk because a girlfriend broke up with him via a public message, then put a video of how she cheated on him, Kyle decided crashing Twitter is an awesome idea. Yeah, post prison, Kyle can say exactly what kind of an idea that was. And it rhymes with numb. So, now he's all for hookups. But now he sees Rylann, whom he likes a lot, but she's a prosecutor... But they really need to talk. About that night...<br /><br />Rylann thinks Kyle is off limits, but well, who could resist those dimples? So, she gets involved, but the question is-what now? I liked Rylann and her plans. She's great.<br /><br />Still, there were too many things going on in the book, there really had to be more Kyle and Rylann. The flirting and bantering is great, but a bigger conflict, and more time and getting to know each other would be better. There was real depth here, though.<br /><br /><i>"His chest pulled almost uncomfortably tight as he pulled her into his arms. “I love you, Rylann.” He cupped her face, peering down into her eyes. “And now I finally have a good answer to the one question everyone always asks me—why I hacked into Twitter. I didn’t know it at the time…but I did it to find you again.”<br />She leaned into him, curling her fingers around his shirt. “That may be the best justification I’ve ever heard for committing a crime.” She looked up at him, her eyes shining. “And I love you, too, you know.”</i><br /><br />Awwww. Kyle *sighs*<br /><br /><br />Oh, I also loved Rae and Rylann's friendship...<br /><br /><i>"Actually, no. The hell with that.” Rylann reached across the table and squeezed Rae’s hand. “Just because we haven’t met Mr. Right doesn’t mean we’re doing anything wrong. And by the way, you’re brilliant and awesome, too. If I were a lesbian, I’d totally settle down with you and make lots of in vitro babies.” </i><br /><br />Hmm, okay :)<br /><br />And Nick is great...<br /><br /><i>“Wonderful. Now I’ve got two of you all up in my business,” Kyle said dryly.<br />Nick slapped him across the shoulders, seeming to thoroughly enjoy this. “Get used to it, Sawyer. That’s what family is for.”</i><br /><br />All in all, not disappointed, exactly, since JJ can write a menu and I'd read it with a smile(which wouldn't leave my face the whole book!), but I wanted more length and story-wise. It's definitely sexy, funny and touching, though, so...READ IT!<br /><br /></span>

Ms. James is one of those authors who <b>‘writes great heroines’</b> – and Rylann Pierce is certainly such a specimen. Some people described her as snarky (or boring); I found her intelligent and articulate. <br/><br/>Ooops! I did something I rarely do and pe</span>
  <span id="freeText5710917535402427539" style="display:none"><i>Usually in sleek, black business suits for court, here is Rylann in worn flannel.</i> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Those who have read the book will know why. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>★★★★½ Enjoyed this one a lot, despite it being a bit chick-lit-ish (not my usual genre). Ms. James is one of those authors who <b>‘writes great heroines’</b> – and Rylann Pierce is certainly such a specimen. Some people described her as snarky (or boring); I found her intelligent and articulate. <br><br>Ooops! I did something I rarely do and peeped at that end, which caused me to set down this volume. Still, I enjoyed the story when I came back to it later, reading late into the night; that’s saying something, when a book can still hold your attention after that.<br><br><br><i>FBI/US Attorney Series</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6642402.Something_About_You__FBI___US_Attorney____1_" title="Something About You (FBI / US Attorney, # 1) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_164493976" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/164493976" />
    <a title="Jess" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1255781-jess"><img alt="Jess" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1502336592p2/1255781.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/164493976?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess" href="/user/show/1255781-jess">Jess</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1255781-jess?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1255781-jess?shelf=for_review">for_review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer164493976" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8633388411816276681">Review posted: <a href='http://happilyeverafter-reads.blogspot.com/2012/04/review-about-that-night-by-julie-james.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Happily Ever After - Reads</a><br/><br/> <b>“There are probably a lot of things bad-boy ex-cons don’t know about good-girl prosecutors.”</b> <br/><br/>Smug Dimples, Prosecutrix Pierce, Meth Lab Rylann and the Twitter Terrorist (or my favorite version of this that comes up El Twitter Terrorista) are all nicknames that our hero and heroine are called during ABOUT THAT NIGHT and it’s the way these nicknames are used during the quick, witty banter that Kyle and Rylann have that drew me right in. What stood out the </span>
  <span id="freeText8633388411816276681" style="display:none">Review posted: <a href="http://happilyeverafter-reads.blogspot.com/2012/04/review-about-that-night-by-julie-james.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Happily Ever After - Reads</a><br /><br /> <b>“There are probably a lot of things bad-boy ex-cons don’t know about good-girl prosecutors.”</b> <br /><br />Smug Dimples, Prosecutrix Pierce, Meth Lab Rylann and the Twitter Terrorist (or my favorite version of this that comes up El Twitter Terrorista) are all nicknames that our hero and heroine are called during ABOUT THAT NIGHT and it’s the way these nicknames are used during the quick, witty banter that Kyle and Rylann have that drew me right in. What stood out the most as I was reading was that there’s no huge angst our couple needs to overcome. This is about two people dealing with their pasts, finding a balance in the present with their careers and figuring out a way to be together for the long haul. It’s incredibly enjoyable, and Julie James keeps hitting it just right on all levels - humor, story, sexiness - with her FBI series.<br /><br />Kyle was first introduced in A LOT LIKE LOVE when we find out that not only is he Jordan’s twin, but most recently, he became the Twitter Terrorist, labeled as such by the Assistant U.S. Attorney (AUSA) handling his case at the time. There’s a chapter early on when Kyle recounts the time leading up to and right after his drunken, broken heart takes down Twitter for 48 hours. When he finds himself in Tijuana trying to drown his sorrows, he also finds himself on the news as a wanted man. He boards a plane back to the U.S to face the music and is immediately taken into custody on the plane:<br /><br /> <b>…Kyle watched as two men wearing standard-issue government suits – clearly FBI agents – boarded the plane and handed over a document to the pilot. <br /><br /> “Yep, that would be me,” Kyle said, grabbing his backpack from underneath the seat in front of him. <br /><br /> The elderly Hispanic man sitting next to him lowered his voice to a whisper. “Drugs?” <br /><br /> “Twitter,” Kyle whispered back.</b><br /><br />Kyle ends up in prison for a few months before the events in A LOT LIKE LOVE spring him out and now he’s a free man, needing to find a new purpose in life. He resigned from his father’s software company, but Kyle’s too intelligent and too driven to sit around wallowing in what’s happened. He takes responsibility for everything he did, he learns from it and he writes up a killer business plan for his next venture.<br /><br />Rylann just moved back to Chicago after living in San Francisco with her boyfriend of three years. He up and decides that moving to Rome sounds like the direction he wants his life to go. Rylann…does not. She never felt the butterflies with Jon, but she was happy with him and a change of scenery and moving closer to her best friend Rae is the fresh start she needs. She’s the new AUSA working for Cameron Lynde (SOMETHING ABOUT YOU) and her first case involves handling the motion that frees Kyle; the same Kyle that she kissed nine years ago at college and actually felt the butterflies with. But circumstances outside their control kept them from going on their first planned date and nine years later they’re finally reunited.<br /> <br />After they see each other again in the court room, Rylann needs Kyle’s help, being her witness with another, unrelated case and he agrees. Their relationship doesn’t get going, and can’t, while Kyle is her witness in the case she needs his help with, but that doesn’t keep the sparks from flying. The minute the coast is clear and there are no work conflicts, they stop denying the attraction. Their scenes together are just – HOT. Kyle is one sexy man and Rylann has no trouble keeping up with him, even tormenting him as much as he does her.<br /><br /> <b>With a chuckle, he stood up and pulled off his shirt. All of the rest of his clothes quickly followed, then he climbed onto her bed and stretched out, fully naked and erect. He folded his hands behind his head and watched her. “What do you plan to do with me now?” <br /><br /> A challenge. Rylann pushed off her elbows and stood up, undressing down to her bra and panties. Then she climbed back onto the bed and straddled him once again. “I have a few ideas.” While holding his gaze, she licked her lips. <br /><br /> His eyes instantly turned a deep, smoldering blue. “Counselor…I really like where you’re going with this.”</b><br /><br />Both the leads have issues in their past and present they’re trying to work through. This is more so the case with Kyle. He’ll forever be known as the Twitter Terrorist, but he’s trying to build up a new company and move on with his life, past the one big mistake he admits to and doesn’t try to make excuses for. We get to see him hire new people and grab his first, and surprisingly perfect, new client for his new company. He’s a completely lovable hero who still has a few insecurities when it comes to relationships, considering the public and humiliating way he was dumped the last time he was with someone. But he’s willing to give it a chance again with Rylann and he puts himself out there on the line for her. He’s sexy, funny and he starts to think about what life would be like with Rylann in it permanently and he likes what he sees.<br /> <br />They keep their relationship secret for much of the book, Rylann is concerned about her position as AUSA and how dating the Twitter Terrorist would reflect on her office. If there’s any little bit of angst, it comes from this. She struggles with taking a chance, having always been that person with a 6-month plan, or 3 –year plan. Taking a leap into something new with Kyle takes her some time, and with one of the sweetest gestures in the whole book surrounding a flannel shirt, she makes sure Kyle knows exactly how she feels about him.<br /> <br />Julie James’ FBI series is one of my favorite contemporary series on the shelves. She delivers every, single, time with characters that are so easy to fall in love with and stories that are fun and fast paced. She easily brings past characters into the current book so we get little updates on them as well as having them contribute to the overall story. ABOUT THAT NIGHT is a book that all fans of contemporary romance must check out. Kyle and Rylann’s story is one I’ll be rereading again and without a doubt enjoying it just as much as I did the first time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8633388411816276681" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9933910041192394542">Audiobook: Narrator – Karen White<br/>I enjoyed this narration. Ms. White did a great job of both male/female voices and I never struggled to discern who was speaking with the various characters. I would gladly listen to more audiobooks narrated by her.<br/><br/>I’ve heard nothing but good things about this series so of course instead of starting at the beginning I jumped into the middle.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553729148ra/27276583.gif' width='450' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Nine years ago, Rylann Pierce met Kyle Rhodes and they shared instant chemistry along with their fun barbs and quips. Now th</span>
  <span id="freeText9933910041192394542" style="display:none">Audiobook: Narrator – Karen White<br>I enjoyed this narration. Ms. White did a great job of both male/female voices and I never struggled to discern who was speaking with the various characters. I would gladly listen to more audiobooks narrated by her.<br><br>I’ve heard nothing but good things about this series so of course instead of starting at the beginning I jumped into the middle.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553729148ra/27276583.gif" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nine years ago, Rylann Pierce met Kyle Rhodes and they shared instant chemistry along with their fun barbs and quips. Now they are both living their lives, although each is dealing with their own issues. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553729148i/27276584._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rylann from a broken relationship and Kyle an ex-con with the moniker of the Twitter Terrorist. From the moment they reunite the chemistry flares to life again but her position as an Assistant US Attorney and his as an ex-convict stand between them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553729148i/27276585._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved these characters! Rylann was smart and sharp but never hard or rude. She knew how to get her job done but she was always had a softer side to her. Kyle was trying to put his past mistake behind him and start his own business. He had a quirky sense of humor that complimented Rylann’s. Together they were so freaking cute.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1553729149ra/27276586.gif" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I thought there was going to be some suspense and mystery to this story but while Rylann is working on a case and we do have some of the legalities of that situation, there was nothing here to cause a huge showdown between the characters and a bad guy. It was actually kinda nice as it was unexpected.<br><br>This has a good pace to it and is relatively low angst with the exception of them figuring out how to make their relationship work due to her job and his past incarceration. I loved watching them both as they transitioned from who they were coming into this relationship into individuals who were willing to do whatever it took to make it work. I’m looking forward to listening to the rest of the series as soon as possible.<br><br>Listened via Audible Romance Package<br>Dual POV<br>Safe <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no ow drama; h’s ex comes back and wants to reunite – H finds him at her apartment and while he knows nothing is going on with them, it causes him to make a rash decision that doesn’t end well; H is not a manwhore and has been celibate for months; h is not a virgin and has been celibate for months <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Triggers <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no apparent triggers <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_260330310" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260330310" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/260330310?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer260330310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2601485859415791860">I’m a huge Julie James fan and her previous book, A Lot Like Love was a favorite of mine last year. In that book we meet Kyle, the son of a billionaire, a brilliant computer scientist, and also a prison inmate. Yes the hero of this book is an ex-con. A very sexy, adorable one at that.<br/><br/>Although Kyle is extremely wealthy, he works hard as the vice president of network security for his father’s company. He also plays hard too, and when his supermodel girlfriend dumps him via twitter, and then posts </span>
  <span id="freeText2601485859415791860" style="display:none">I’m a huge Julie James fan and her previous book, A Lot Like Love was a favorite of mine last year. In that book we meet Kyle, the son of a billionaire, a brilliant computer scientist, and also a prison inmate. Yes the hero of this book is an ex-con. A very sexy, adorable one at that.<br /><br />Although Kyle is extremely wealthy, he works hard as the vice president of network security for his father’s company. He also plays hard too, and when his supermodel girlfriend dumps him via twitter, and then posts a video of her making out with a random dude in a hot tub, Kyle get a little upset. He decides to throw a virus at Twitter, which shuts it down for 48 hours. Although he is a computer genius, the government also has computer geniuses at their disposal, and soon the FBI tracks him down on his way home from Tijuana<br /><br /><i>Sitting eight rows back, Kyle watched as two men wearing standard issue government suits – clearly FBI agents – boarded the plane and handed over a document to the pilot.<br />“Yep, that would be me,” Kyle said, grabbing his backpack from underneath the seat in front of him.<br />The elderly Hispanic man sitting next to him lowered his voice to a whisper. “Drugs?”<br />“Twitter,” Kyle whispered back.</i><br /><br />The US Attorney’s office go after him hard, and label him the “Twitter Terrorist” and he gets sentenced to 18 months in a federal prison. If you’ve read the previous book, A Lot Like Love, you know that his sister helps the FBI with a different case and in return, he only has to serve four months. Kyle openly admits to making a mistake and takes full responsibility for his actions. Being wealthy and sexy, his story makes national news and people either think his stunt is hilarious or they throw rude gestures at him every where he goes.<br /><br />Nine years before all of this happens, he briefly meets Rylann Pierce at a bar. Totally smitten with her they both share a kiss and plan to go out on a date but that date never happens. Kyle goes on with his life and work and Rylann finishes law school and moves to San Francisco to start her career. But in present day when her boyfriend decides to move to Rome, something Rylann is totally not interested in, she decides to pack it up and move back home to Chicago. It’s hard for her, she likes to have a plan in her life and moving back to Chicago is a big step. She lands a job as an Assistant US Attorney and guess what her first court appointment has to deal with? Yes, the Twitter Terrorist. Kyle has to go to court for the judge to approve his early release, and Rylann fills in for the original lawyer. They both remember each other and that steamy kiss they shared nine years prior.<br /><br />Expecting to never see Kyle again after this, when the FBI comes to her with a murder at the prison Kyle was in, she knows she will be seeing more of him. Kyle may have overheard an important conversation relating to this murder, and now she must convince him to testify, although he is definitely not on good terms with her department.<br /><br />Julie James writes such smart books. She seamlessly combines courtroom drama and legal issues into a very sexy romance, with witty dialogue and hot bedroom scenes. The first half of this book is background into Kyle and Rylann’s lives and the two of them working together on this FBI case. Because he is a witness in her investigation, ethically she really can’t pursue a relationship with him. Although Kyle has sworn off serious dating since his last break-up, Rylann in her business suits and serious demeanor just turns him on. And Rylann knows dating an ex-con might not be the best career move she ever made, but she just can’t get him out of her mind. She likes to plan out her life, and she isn’t sure how Kyle fits into that plan.The build-up to their relationship is done quite well.<br /><br />Once we get into the bedroom, I think this is the sexiest book of Julie James’s yet. We get several love scenes, and the wait for them made them that much better. I love that these are are mature – they don’t fight about petty things. They tease each other and flirt so cute. Kyle is just down right charming and I adore that he never comes across as a rich, spoiled son. He takes responsibility for his actions and works hard to make his life better.<br /><br />The supporting characters including Rae, Rylann’s best friend and Jordan, Kyle’s sister are fun additions to this book too. I also like how supportive Kyle’s family is to him. Although his father isn’t pleased when his son lands in prison, there isn’t big family drama surrounding him. Rylann is close with her parents as well, which is refreshing.<br /><br />About That Night is a smart, fun and sexy book. Although it can be a stand alone, I highly recommend the previous book in the series, A Lot Like Love.<br /><br />Rating: B+</span>
  <a data-text-id="2601485859415791860" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
