<div id="review_2215055923" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2215055923" />
    <a title="Chan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48867675-chan"><img alt="Chan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537488132p2/48867675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2215055923?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chan" href="/user/show/48867675-chan">Chan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2215055923" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5685437343345534319"><b>Writing</b>: I like Julie James’ writing style. She knows how to hold her readers attention. 2 POVs. 3rd Person narration.<br/><br/><b>Characters</b>: Rylann and Kyle are the MCs. Rylann’s personality was similar to Cameron’s in book 1. Kyle was a great character, but his transition into maturity was not that great. I had to remind myself he was no longer that immature kid.<br/><br/><b>Storyline</b>: Book 2 informs us that Kyle has committed a horrible (albeit funny) crime. In book 3 we get more details on the crime. We also meet Ry</span>
  <span id="freeText5685437343345534319" style="display:none"><b>Writing</b>: I like Julie James’ writing style. She knows how to hold her readers attention. 2 POVs. 3rd Person narration.<br /><br /><b>Characters</b>: Rylann and Kyle are the MCs. Rylann’s personality was similar to Cameron’s in book 1. Kyle was a great character, but his transition into maturity was not that great. I had to remind myself he was no longer that immature kid.<br /><br /><b>Storyline</b>: Book 2 informs us that Kyle has committed a horrible (albeit funny) crime. In book 3 we get more details on the crime. We also meet Rylann who is in Law School and meets the bad boy billionaire in a bar. Rylann and Kyle create sparks, but life keeps them from each other for 9 years. They meet up with each other in a very unexpected way and try to recapture what was lost. <br /><br />I’m enjoying this series, but was disappointed with this book. Julie James kept making it seem like there was danger lurking around the corner, BUT NOTHING HAPPENED. Nobody was in danger of anything. <br /><br />You should never tease an action junkie like that. It’s just wrong. I felt shortchanged. This also dampened my enjoyment of the book. I was constantly waiting for something to happen and before I knew it, the book was over. <br /><br /><b>Intimacy Scenes</b>: This was better than expected. Kyle wore his emotions on his sleeves and was pretty easy going, but in the bedroom...the beta in him disappeared.<br /><br /><b>Overall</b>: Although I enjoyed the book, I was also disappointed. The first two books had a little suspense and action. This book was set up perfectly for the same, but it fell flat. I’ll read book 4 and hope Julie James brings the action</span>

<div id="review_242282168" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3192922-saly?shelf=cops-law-enforcement-security">cops-law-enforcement-security</a>,

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1066300776677329173"><b>Rating 3.5</b><br/><br/>I've been waiting for this story since last year because who doesn't love reading about a billionaire that looks like Sawyer from LOST and downed twitter when his girlfriend dumped him publicly? I say awesome setup and it was and Kyle was totally yummy.<br/><br/>Kyle and Rylann met nine years ago and had a connection and a date which never went anywhere because Kyle's mom died and Rylann became a lawyer and followed her career plan to the T. Kyle never did his PhD.D and went to work at his fathe</span>
  <span id="freeText1066300776677329173" style="display:none"><b>Rating 3.5</b><br /><br />I've been waiting for this story since last year because who doesn't love reading about a billionaire that looks like Sawyer from LOST and downed twitter when his girlfriend dumped him publicly? I say awesome setup and it was and Kyle was totally yummy.<br /><br />Kyle and Rylann met nine years ago and had a connection and a date which never went anywhere because Kyle's mom died and Rylann became a lawyer and followed her career plan to the T. Kyle never did his PhD.D and went to work at his father's company, working and partying hard and he did make an effort to get serious relationship wise but it ended up with him getting drunk, shutting twitter and spending four months in jail and his twin Jordan bailing him out, so he is done trying to make a commitment and with one meeting should be free of the US Attorney office.<br /><br />Rylann has just moved to Chicago and joined the AUSA's office. She broke up with her boyfriend of three years, six months ago when he decided to move to Rome and she refused to follow him since it didn't go with her plans. So, while Kyle is about spontaneity Rylann is all about her plans and her career and they meet again nine years later in the court-room and are thrown together again when Rylann's needs his help in a case related to prison going-on's.<br /><br />I liked that Rylann maintained her professionalism and despite the sparks between them nothing happened till he was a witness in her case. If I had to grade this book it would be for Kyle only, he was funny, romantic and loyal to his family. He had accepted responsibility for what he did and made something out of it by following his heart and opening his own venture.<br /><br />I was a little luke-worm about Rylann, she just seemed like one of those women with plans and she wanted to keep her and Kyle under wraps since they would be a source for gossip and she didn't want that to adversely affect her job and I got that, that her job was important and that Kyle moved at a faster pace than her but nobody likes being kept like a guilty secret and I loved that Kyle told her that and that she had to make a choice and decided if personal happiness too was important.<br /><br />This book was way hotter than any other Julie James book but for me that is not a consideration and I felt while attempting to make the book sexy, maybe it wasn't that sexy and it was just trying way too hard to be, even now Just the Sexiest Man Alive remains a favorite of mine, the reasons being I could feel the sexual tension, in this book it wasn't that center-stage and I was supposed to be feeling it and I didn't.<br /><br />As a contemporary romance this book is worth trying but I just felt as if a magical spark was missing.</span>

I have a job where I have to disclose stuff. I do so unreservedly. What a dumb risk. <br /><br />Anyway, that's not really the point. <div id="review_2312591459" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2312591459" />
    <a title="Camilla Isley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32921088-camilla-isley"><img alt="Camilla Isley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444931510p2/32921088.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/199694495?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sheryl C. Nash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sheryl C. Nash" href="/user/show/6039696-sheryl-c-nash">Sheryl C. Nash</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6039696-sheryl-c-nash?shelf=romance-erotica">romance-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6039696-sheryl-c-nash?shelf=romance-contemporary">romance-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6039696-sheryl-c-nash?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer199694495" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4055235012633157283">One million stars!! What? Yup, you read right. In all my 1000+ reviews on Goodreads, the most i have credited to an author was either 10 stars or 100 stars, but this book exceeded my expectations AND THEN SOME! I'm sure we have all been excited for a book, only for it to fall flat when we finally got our hands on it, well... About That Night is NOT ONE OF THOSE BOOKS!!! I was DYING to read about Kyle Rhodes when i met him in the previous book in the FBI series;<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___2_' title='A Lot Like Love (FBI, #2) by Julie James' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Lot Like Love</a> ... here was guy wh</span>
  <span id="freeText4055235012633157283" style="display:none">One million stars!! What? Yup, you read right. In all my 1000+ reviews on Goodreads, the most i have credited to an author was either 10 stars or 100 stars, but this book exceeded my expectations AND THEN SOME! I'm sure we have all been excited for a book, only for it to fall flat when we finally got our hands on it, well... About That Night is NOT ONE OF THOSE BOOKS!!! I was DYING to read about Kyle Rhodes when i met him in the previous book in the FBI series;<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___2_" title="A Lot Like Love (FBI, #2) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">A Lot Like Love</a> ... here was guy who was a nerd, but not... Suffice to say he captured my imagination and waiting for over 9+ months to read his story just did my head in... <br /><br />Kyle...sigh what can i say? Funny, hot, sexy, sweet as hell, sexy, hot... right said those already.. and Rylann (chicken wing girl...LOVED that reference!!) was intelligent and snarky but underneath it all she was really unsure of what to do and i for one am so glad she embraced her inner bad girl and took a chance with Kyle... all the pent up frustration between those two, just made their coming together at halfway through the book SMOKIN' HOT!<br /><br />If you haven't read the previous 2 books in this series, i would say read them before reading this, especially the previous book; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___2_" title="A Lot Like Love (FBI, #2) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">A Lot Like Love</a> as you will understand a bit about Kyle's background and what happened. <br /><br />SIGH... in conclusion, Ms. James; BEST BOOK EVER!!! Now please excuse me, while i go have some "dreams" about Kyle... :)</span>

<div id="review_193698890" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/193698890" />
    <a title="Anne OK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok"><img alt="Anne OK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505981069p2/285610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/193698890?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne OK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne OK" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok">Anne OK</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/285610-anne-ok?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer193698890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer135403892279725652">“About That Night” made my day! Sometimes this reader just wants a contemporary romance that is filled with feel-good feelings, smartly written dialogue, sexy romance, and charming characters to win my heart. That’s exactly what Julie James’s latest release provided in spades. I read it from cover to cover without moving out of my chair. <br/><br/>Our hero isn’t thinking clearly when he strikes out to settle a score and crashes Twitter. Soon he finds himself being escorted off an airplane by FBI agents an</span>
  <span id="freeText135403892279725652" style="display:none">“About That Night” made my day! Sometimes this reader just wants a contemporary romance that is filled with feel-good feelings, smartly written dialogue, sexy romance, and charming characters to win my heart. That’s exactly what Julie James’s latest release provided in spades. I read it from cover to cover without moving out of my chair. <br /><br />Our hero isn’t thinking clearly when he strikes out to settle a score and crashes Twitter. Soon he finds himself being escorted off an airplane by FBI agents and charged with multiple felonies. After his release from prison, he finds no comfort in being labeled an ex-con and as the “Twitter Terrorist.” But even more complications arise when he goes and falls in love with a federal prosecutor involved in his case. And wouldn’t you know it, she doesn’t think her career goals will survive a love connection between an “ex-con” and a “federal prosecutor. Ah – but this ex-con is not only a real charmer with dimples, he’s determined, rich, smart, and quite simply irresistible. <br /><br />In this installment of her FBI series, Ms. James turns up the heat and it is a welcomed addition. Kyle and Rylann have great chemistry. Kyle is a smart and charming. Rylann is strong and witty. They approach their relationship as equals. It’s fun to watch them spar, tease and tempt one another. Their attraction to each other is never questioned. <br /><br />Not a major concern but it caught my attention and made me wonder: Why this cover of the series, in particular, had its female model clothed in a pantsuit. It didn’t hold true to the storyline. Rylann’s business suit skirts were not only a turn-on to Kyle throughout the book but also source for the FBI’s nickname for her. <br /><br />After such a marvelous story, the ending was a bit abrupt. I wish there had been a little more spice in the happily-ever-after. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="135403892279725652" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_164083017" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/164083017" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3125133-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1264894304p2/3125133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/164083017?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/3125133-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=2readseries">2readseries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3125133-amy?shelf=fv-review">fv-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer164083017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16656721370229492854"><br/><br/><b>@KyleRhodes</b><br/><br/><br/><b>Profile:</b> Blonde billionaire heir with a love for flannel, exceptional wine, and likes his women hot and spicy just like his chicken wings; hater of all things Victoria’s Secret.<br/><br/><b>Hashtags:</b> #SmugDimples, #HotandSpicy, #TwitterTerrorist<br/><br/><b>Trending:</b> # Prosecutrix Pierce, #Counselor, #Meth Lab Rylann,<br/><br/>Call it fate or two ships crossing in the night, but that is exactly how Kyle Rhodes, son to billionaire Grey Rhodes, has stumbled upon Rylann Pierce in a bar celebrating her grad student status a</span>
  <span id="freeText16656721370229492854" style="display:none"><br /><br /><b>@KyleRhodes</b><br /><br /><br /><b>Profile:</b> Blonde billionaire heir with a love for flannel, exceptional wine, and likes his women hot and spicy just like his chicken wings; hater of all things Victoria’s Secret.<br /><br /><b>Hashtags:</b> #SmugDimples, #HotandSpicy, #TwitterTerrorist<br /><br /><b>Trending:</b> # Prosecutrix Pierce, #Counselor, #Meth Lab Rylann,<br /><br />Call it fate or two ships crossing in the night, but that is exactly how Kyle Rhodes, son to billionaire Grey Rhodes, has stumbled upon Rylann Pierce in a bar celebrating her grad student status and temporary respite before heading off to law school. Never one to be shy, Kyle engages Rylann in conversation doing his best to charm her with his piercing blue eyes and sexy dimples. Sparks immediately fly for both and when the night wraps and Rylann is left alone, Kyle offers to walk her home. After much flirting and teasing from both, Rylann ends the night taking an unforgettable kiss as well as agreeing to a date for beer and chicken wings with the persistent Kyle Rhodes. But fate intervenes again as tragedy strikes the Rhodes family and their date never transpires.<br /><br /><i>“There are some things a girl never forgets. And one of those is a kiss from the right guy.”</i><br /><br />Fast forward nine years later and Rylann has moved to Chicago to start her new position as Assistant U.S. Attorney. Kyle Rhodes is serving his last week on home arrest after being convicted for hacking and shutting down the social media website, Twitter for 48 hours. After an agreed motion is set for court and the hearing starts, Kyle is shocked to see that the federal prosecutor on his case is none other than Rylann Pierce. And what do you know…the spark is still there for both of them. Thanks to the motion set forth by the U.S. Attorney’s office, Kyle is once again a free man and now knows he has unfinished business with one sassy federal prosecutor. Circumstances are in his favor, as Kyle is approached to be a witness in Rylann’s investigation into a prison murder and he is all too happy to assist. Rylann knows that she cannot ethically pursue a relationship with Kyle Rhodes while he is a witness to her case, but that does not damper the feelings of desire she has for the ex-con. And for someone who plans her life to a tee, Rylann has no clue what will happen once the case is over. What she does know is that she doesn’t want Kyle walking out of her life a second time and she makes that clear the night he is no longer her witness.<br /><br />There are a handful of authors that have the eagerly anticipated once a year release that you are dying for and Julie James is at the top my list. Ever since I discovered Ms. James and her sexy FBI man Jack Pallas, from Something About You, I immediately claimed him as mine and became a fan girl of the engaging contemporary author.<br /><br />The best off the cuff way to describe James is a “sure thing” for a captivating, sexy, contemporary read. Ms. James seasons her FBI series with her own personal knowledge of the legal world and then develops sizzling and enticing characters to live and find love within the pages. Kyle really grabbed my heart early on. Although he is a billionaire, he doesn’t flaunt it, nor does he have the attitude of the typical “trust fund baby”. He is a hard worker, desiring to build a career outside of his father’s business and ultimately desiring to “pay it forward” as a result of past mistakes. What is evident early on is under the self-assured cockiness and wit he exudes while trying to “get the girl” there is also a hit of insecurity in himself as well as a fear of committed relationships given his past failures. Those moments of vulnerability make him all the more adorable.<br /><br />Kyle is considerate, thoughtful, sentimental, witty, and embodies every woman’s dream of the quintessential male. Rylann is a strong, assured woman driven to succeed in what many would consider a “man’s domain”. She is a planner, sets solid goals and is not one to “fly by the seat of her pants” under any circumstance. So, what is refreshing to see is how Kyle breaks down some of that rigidness in his relentless pursuit and down right flusters her to the point that she’s unable to stay on her designated track. His mischievous and honest pursuit of Rylann combine with the intense sexual tension that radiates from both is enamoring to watch and as the reader, I didn’t want their story to end!<br /><br />About that Night is a sexy, sizzling addition to the FBI series and while it can stand alone, it is more gratifying to know the characters from the prior two books that interact with both Kyle and Rylann. Kyle is a total swoon worthy hero as well as Jack Pallas and Nick McCall. Trust me when I say you will not be disappointed! So to sum it up I leave you with my tweet to Julie James upon finishing the book:<br /><br /><b>@juljames</b> Oh Julie, you’ve gone and done it now. Jack Pallas is my lighter fluid &amp; now Kyle Rhodes has arrived and torched my heart! *swoon*<br /><br /><br /><br />Kyle Rhodes aka "Twitter Terrorist" was originally posted at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.fictionvixen.com/2012/04/review-about-that-night-by-julie-james.html">http://www.fictionvixen.com/2012/04/r...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16656721370229492854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2388840075" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2388840075" />
    <a title="Obsidian" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35942740-obsidian"><img alt="Obsidian" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509845837p2/35942740.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2388840075?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Obsidian" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Obsidian" href="/user/show/35942740-obsidian">Obsidian</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39124046-about-that-night">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2388840075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2733200918853928718">This will be fairly short. I didn't like this one. Seriously. The plot was ridiculous and I am sorry I could not really get over a woman with an important job like Rylann's would be okay with her dating a former criminal. Then again it's a new day in the world and white collar crimes seem to just be getting ignored right now. That said, I didn't really like the male lead Kyle at all. I thought the two of them didn't really fit and thought the book focused too much on Nick and Jordan from book #2</span>
  <span id="freeText2733200918853928718" style="display:none">This will be fairly short. I didn't like this one. Seriously. The plot was ridiculous and I am sorry I could not really get over a woman with an important job like Rylann's would be okay with her dating a former criminal. Then again it's a new day in the world and white collar crimes seem to just be getting ignored right now. That said, I didn't really like the male lead Kyle at all. I thought the two of them didn't really fit and thought the book focused too much on Nick and Jordan from book #2 for my taste. <br /><br />"About That Night" has Rylann Pierce coming face to face with the guy she hasn't seen in 9 years after having an epic meet-cute, billionaire heir, Kyle Rhodes. Now that Rylann is working for the U.S. Attorney's office, she is in charge of wrapping up Kyle's criminal case. Initially brushing him off, she ends up having to seek him out again when another case comes up that needs Kyle's help. <br /><br />I thought the whole Kyle is a witness that needs to help out the U.S. Attorney's could have been done better. I thought that James just rushed to wrap up that plot-line. The rest of the book was just Kyle and Rylann being together and they were not a big enough draw for me after a while. I think that James included so much from Jordan and Nick since there was not enough to hang a whole book on with these two. <br /><br />The sex scenes were meh. Ultimately this book is mostly about Rylann having to decide between her job and Kyle, and I was all for her dumping Kyle. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2733200918853928718" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1679501932" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5252054-irena"><img alt="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425497470p2/5252054.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1679501932?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ᴥ Irena ᴥ" href="/user/show/5252054-irena">ᴥ Irena ᴥ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5252054-irena?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1679501932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1010510401742094929"><b>3.5</b><br/><br/>When I wrote that I wouldn't mind Kyle's story I didn't know I'd get it in the next book. I'm not complaining. I loved Kyle.<br/>If you read the series in order, you already know what happened to him and why.<br/><br/>Unlike the first two books though, this one has almost zero suspense. Yes, there is a case at first but it really serves only one purpose - to give Kyle and Rylann an opportunity to meet again. <br/><i>About That Night</i> is a light romance and one could find things to nitpick, but I won't. It was fun an</span>
  <span id="freeText1010510401742094929" style="display:none"><b>3.5</b><br /><br />When I wrote that I wouldn't mind Kyle's story I didn't know I'd get it in the next book. I'm not complaining. I loved Kyle.<br />If you read the series in order, you already know what happened to him and why.<br /><br />Unlike the first two books though, this one has almost zero suspense. Yes, there is a case at first but it really serves only one purpose - to give Kyle and Rylann an opportunity to meet again. <br /><i>About That Night</i> is a light romance and one could find things to nitpick, but I won't. It was fun and very low on angst. It's because nothing bad happened between them nine years ago, nobody was abused or hurt or something similar. Neither needs healing and that's exactly what I needed to read. The bad things that did happen are connected to something or someone else. <br />The humour I expected was there too.<br /> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b> "You don't think it's too much? Like I'm trying too hard?"<br />Jordan put her hand over her heart again. "Oh, it's like watching Bambi take his first steps."</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Anyway, even though I prefer more suspense, I enjoyed this book. <blockquote>
  <b>"But you're supposed to be the girl with the plan." "Funny enough, I always seem to forget that around you," Rylann whispered.</b>
</blockquote><br /></span>

<div id="review_442070528" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/442070528" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/442070528?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=lol">lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer442070528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4473462452229851552">Another fantastic instalment in Julie James’ FBI/US Attorney series! This time, the story is about Rylann Pierce, Assistant US Attorney, and billionaire-heir, computer genius, ex-con and gorgeously sexy Kyle Rhodes (brother of Jordan, the heroine from book 2 - <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___US_Attorney___2_' title='A Lot Like Love (FBI / US Attorney, #2) by Julie James' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Lot Like Love</a>). <br/><br/>Rylann and Kyle meet as Grad Students one night in a bar, and with an instant physical attraction and sensational banter, there is some serious chemistry between them. They make plans to meet up the following night, but K</span>
  <span id="freeText4473462452229851552" style="display:none">Another fantastic instalment in Julie James’ FBI/US Attorney series! This time, the story is about Rylann Pierce, Assistant US Attorney, and billionaire-heir, computer genius, ex-con and gorgeously sexy Kyle Rhodes (brother of Jordan, the heroine from book 2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8419428.A_Lot_Like_Love__FBI___US_Attorney___2_" title="A Lot Like Love (FBI / US Attorney, #2) by Julie James" rel="nofollow noopener">A Lot Like Love</a>). <br /><br />Rylann and Kyle meet as Grad Students one night in a bar, and with an instant physical attraction and sensational banter, there is some serious chemistry between them. They make plans to meet up the following night, but Kyle never shows. He has an excellent reason (not that Rylann knows this at the time), but their lives take drastically different paths from that point, and they don’t see each other again. <br /><br />Until nine years later... Rylann has recently returned to Chicago looking for a fresh start following the break up of a long term relationship, and she is now an Assistant US Attorney. She and Kyle run into each other again in Court following his early release from prison for a hilarious case of ‘cyber-terrorism’. And from the instant their eyes meet, the sparks are still there.<br /><br /><i>“Kyle remembered that smile. He’d once walked up to a complete stranger in a bar because of one just like it. And had then been thoroughly sassed.”</i><br /><br />Things get complicated when Kyle becomes a key witness in Rylann’s next big case, and the two of them are forced to spend time together. They are both clearly still attracted to each other, but Rylann is ethically unable to enter into anything with a witness. The case takes up a big portion of the first half of this book, and there’s not a heap of time with them together, but when they are, the banter flies, and the UST builds to dangerous levels, and I was getting antsy waiting for something to happen. Once the case is done though, it’s all on with this line…<br /><br /><i>“Nine years ago, I walked up to the most beautiful girl in the bar, and tonight she's still the only person I want to talk to.”</i><br /><br />Oh yeah! Unleash the steamy!!! Kyle and Jordan are smokin’ hot together. They are both very self-assured and confident, and hilariously sarcastic, and from the very beginning they are both open and honest about what they want - there are no games, no stupid, and it’s awesome! And, of course, the quips and one-liners still fly fast…<br /><br /><i>“His gaze shifted to the wild bush sprouting from her head. “Wow. Did I do that to your hair?” He looked oddly pleased at the thought.<br />Rylann made a mental note to throw a flat iron in her purse the next time she had sex in the shower with a billionaire ex-con. Not that there was going to be a next time. “Not all of us are lucky enough to have freakishly perfect, shampoo-commercial hair. This is what happens when I get wet.”<br />His expression turned wicked. “I know exactly what happens when you get wet, counselor.”<br />Yep, she’d walked right into that one.<br />“Usually there’s a lot of moaning and heavy breathing,” he continued. “Although my favourite part is the way you say my name-“<br />“Kyle,” she interrupted, glaring at him. <br />“Nope, not like that. A bit more fiery and enthusiastic.” He patted the bed next to him. “Let’s work on it until we get it perfect.”</i><br /><br />In the beginning both of them are adamant that they don’t want a relationship, but it doesn’t take long before emotions become involved, and even though there are issues between them that need to be resolved, there are some gorgeously tender and romantic moments. <br /><br /><i>“You came along and changed everything. I don’t want to be some guy you’re fooling around with anymore, Rylann. I want to be with you all the way.”</i><br /><br />As with other books in the series, this is a fast-paced, fun, romantic read with heaps of one liners that had me chuckling all the way through. There is a strong cast of characters, including the couples from the previous books, and although the romance didn’t seem as prominent through the whole book as it has been in the others, it was still really well paced, and I loved Kyle and Rylann’s story.<br /><br />4 stars. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4473462452229851552" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_193494882" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/193494882" />
    <a title="Nisha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2451459-nisha"><img alt="Nisha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473558883p2/2451459.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/193494882?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nisha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nisha" href="/user/show/2451459-nisha">Nisha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=kickass-heroine">kickass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2451459-nisha?shelf=crime">crime</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer193494882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13954459388900235831">Most of you already know how obsessed I am with Julie James, so it comes to no one's surprise that I actually BOUGHT this ebook right after it's release. So, I paid full price, been drooling over Kyle since the last book, and it's Julie James - obviously, I went in with high expectations. Maybe it was because of those high expectations, but I was a little disappointed with About That Night.<br/><br/>Nine years ago, before Kyle Rhodes, became the Twitter Terrorist, he met a law student named Rylann Pierce </span>
  <span id="freeText13954459388900235831" style="display:none">Most of you already know how obsessed I am with Julie James, so it comes to no one's surprise that I actually BOUGHT this ebook right after it's release. So, I paid full price, been drooling over Kyle since the last book, and it's Julie James - obviously, I went in with high expectations. Maybe it was because of those high expectations, but I was a little disappointed with About That Night.<br /><br />Nine years ago, before Kyle Rhodes, became the Twitter Terrorist, he met a law student named Rylann Pierce at a bar. They hit it off almost immediately, but before they got a chance to have a first date, Kyle's mother dies. In the present day, Rylann has moved on with her life and has become a highly successful prosecutor. As the new member of the US Attorney office, Rylann and Kyle reunite in the courtroom. After fumbling through official business, the pair finally begin their elicit relationship, but can an ambitious Prosecutor and Ex-con really have a future?<br /><br />Of course. It helps that said ex-con happens to be a hot, socially competent millionaire computer genius.<br /><br />Kyle Rhodes is adorable. He's the nicest, cutest hero Julie James has ever created and while apparently he was a playboy...I don't see it. He's also really motivated to fix his life after making a really dumb mistake. That's really sexy. Rylann's a tough cookie, but unlike our previous heroines, she was missing something that made her memorable. She was likeable though and I could relate to her, so I guess I don't mind. The only flaw with this book is the chemistry. <br /><br />I know what you're all thinking, 'How can you still rate this 4 stars when the chemistry was failing?' Well, I was comparing it with Ms. James's previous books, where the couple verbally sparred through the majority of the book, until finally falling into bed. In this one, Kyle and Rylann sparred in their flashback and tiptoed around each other in the professional capacity, but otherwise, they were very cordial to each other and had multiple steamy romantic encounters (about mid-way through the book). And while I am no prude, the graphic nature of the bedroom scenes detracted from Ms. James's ability to build the characters' budding sexual tension.<br /><br />Otherwise, this was a cute book. There was some comedy, but it was primarily around Kyle and his people (Dex and Jordan). Rylann didn't really have much charisma despite being quite likeable. Anyway, it wasn't exactly a memorable book, but it didn't feel like a waste of time, so I can still recommend it.<br /><br />Btw, I can see why a great guy would fall for a nice girl like Rylann, but I want him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13954459388900235831" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6010848203082366210">I have already read one book in this series. The series that as far as I know is very popular and enjoyed by the readers. And again, like with the previous book I read, I liked it and at the same time I’m a bit disappointed.<br/><br/>Well, I’m a huge fan of romantic suspense and this is definitely not a romantic suspense story. I knew it from the very beginning and I wasn’t surprised. But it doesn’t change the fact that I sooo wanted it to be more suspenseful. There are some perfect opportunities. Rylann </span>
  <span id="freeText6010848203082366210" style="display:none">I have already read one book in this series. The series that as far as I know is very popular and enjoyed by the readers. And again, like with the previous book I read, I liked it and at the same time I’m a bit disappointed.<br /><br />Well, I’m a huge fan of romantic suspense and this is definitely not a romantic suspense story. I knew it from the very beginning and I wasn’t surprised. But it doesn’t change the fact that I sooo wanted it to be more suspenseful. There are some perfect opportunities. Rylann is working on a case of aggressive prison guard! Even knowing perfectly well that it is just a plain contemporary romance, I totally expected that this topic would be used somehow. When it did not happen and the book ended, I was like: well… that’s all?! So yes, I want this book to be so much more.<br /><br />But at the same time I generally enjoyed the story. Or maybe the characters. They are complicated, three0dimansional and well-developed. It’s nice to follow them around. They are strong characters and a quite matching pair. <br /><br />The idea of a second chance romance is introduced in a very good manner. And who hasn’t got a soft spot for this motive. The feelings between Rylann and Kyle are pretty believable. They make a nice couple I will be glad to meet in next books. <br /><br />I have so many conflicted feelings about this book. I enjoyed it and at the same time I wish it’s something more! Anyway, this is a pretty nice series.<br /></span>

<div id="review_530355999" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530355999" />
    <a title="Samantha Young" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4394330-samantha-young"><img alt="Samantha Young" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593532204p2/4394330.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/530355999?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha Young" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha Young" href="/user/show/4394330-samantha-young">Samantha Young</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4394330-samantha-young?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530355999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8681979546229995437">Completely addictive, About That Night is smart, funny (the crime Kyle committed, and why, had me in stitches!), witty, sexy and utterly entertaining. Kyle somehow manages to be incredibly hot and offbeat at the same time, and Rylann's sense of humour and self-possession was really refreshing. She was such a likeable heroine. Love it!<br/>Thoroughly enjoyed every minute of the story. Now I'm off to start back at the beginning as I didn't realise this was book 3 (apparently I can't read titles properl</span>
  <span id="freeText8681979546229995437" style="display:none">Completely addictive, About That Night is smart, funny (the crime Kyle committed, and why, had me in stitches!), witty, sexy and utterly entertaining. Kyle somehow manages to be incredibly hot and offbeat at the same time, and Rylann's sense of humour and self-possession was really refreshing. She was such a likeable heroine. Love it!<br />Thoroughly enjoyed every minute of the story. Now I'm off to start back at the beginning as I didn't realise this was book 3 (apparently I can't read titles properly) in the series. Although it should be noted they can be read as standalones. <br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MPdIuOg1kUVHtN1dAmTUmTtOJ/zY+g5mGifw5vtVfc5Z1TDC/etwEpnGU/ZRGYEfysb8QmWYU5iq5nNkklnC+g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XXd4dX9KbWpL/mYWBcMEOVxqwQ1UF0NE0Q74Jj/vXQA0VQAPapSMPZWM6L1WvlG/reIas+l1Hrphz3ukVuPiNA==')})
  }

Then his boss drops a bombshell: Cole has competition. Female competition, in the form of a fresh-faced tomboy who can hang with the dudes—and write circles around them, too. Cole usually likes his women flirty and curvy, but he takes a special interest in his skinny, sassy rival, if only to keep an eye on her. And soon, he can’t take his eyes off her.   Penelope Pope knows all too well that she comes off as just one of the guys. Since she’s learned that wanting more usually leads to disappointment, Penelope’s resigned to sitting on the sidelines when it comes to love. So why does Cole make her want to get back in the game? The man is as arrogant as he is handsome. He probably sees her as nothing more than a barrier to his dream job. But when an unexpected kiss turns into a night of irresistible passion, Penelope has to figure out whether they’re just fooling around—or starting something real.  Includes a special message from the <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer819684626602508672">New York Times bestselling author Julie James practiced law with one of the nation's largest firms for several years until she began writing screenplays. After Hollywood producers optioned two of her scripts, she decided to leave the practice of law to write full-time. Her books have been translated into twenty-two languages and Julie’s ninth novel, THE THING ABOUT LOVE, is now available.<br/><br/>Julie Jam</span>
  <span id="freeText819684626602508672" style="display:none">New York Times bestselling author Julie James practiced law with one of the nation's largest firms for several years until she began writing screenplays. After Hollywood producers optioned two of her scripts, she decided to leave the practice of law to write full-time. Her books have been translated into twenty-two languages and Julie’s ninth novel, THE THING ABOUT LOVE, is now available.<br /><br />Julie James lives with her husband and two children in Chicago, where she is working on her next novel.<br /><br />Visit Julie's Facebook page: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/JulieJamesfanpage">http://www.facebook.com/JulieJamesfan...</a><br /><br />Follow Julie on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://twitter.com/juljames">http://twitter.com/juljames</a> and Instagram: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/juliejamesauthor/">https://www.instagram.com/juliejamesa...</a></span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;I will never, ever regret stopping you from walking out of my life a second time, Kyle," she said in an emotional voice. "And I can prove it."<br />She reached for the buttons on her trench coat and undid them, one at a time. Then she opened the coat and let it drop to the floor.<br />And even if she didn't say a single word more, Kyle knew he would never again doubt the way Rylann felt about him.<br />She was wearing his flannel shirt.<br />"You kept it," he said softly. "All this time."<br />She nodded. "For nine years, I've held on to this darn shirt, literally dragging it across the country and back."<br />Kyle touched her cheek, gently brushing away a tear with his thumb. "Why?"<br />She paused hesitantly, and then with a tender smile, finally put it all on the line, too. "I guess I always hoped you'd come back for it someday.&rdquo;</span>
